\doxysubsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61ac}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61ac}} 
\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiBlendMode@{aiBlendMode}}
\index{aiBlendMode@{aiBlendMode}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiBlendMode}{aiBlendMode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61ac}{ai\+Blend\+Mode}}}



Defines alpha-\/blend flags. 

If you\textquotesingle{}re familiar with Open\+GL or D3D, these flags aren\textquotesingle{}t new to you. They define {\itshape how} the final color value of a pixel is computed, basing on the previous color at that pixel and the new color value from the material. The blend formula is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{SourceColor * SourceBlend + DestColor * DestBlend}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where Dest\+Color is the previous color in the frame-\/buffer at this position and Source\+Color is the material color before the transparency calculation.~\newline
 This corresponds to the \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7e4425c7ac9ca7fc5dfd57069a0839dc}{AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+BLEND\+\_\+\+FUNC}} property. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiBlendMode\_Default@{aiBlendMode\_Default}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiBlendMode\_Default@{aiBlendMode\_Default}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61aca2df47d5d42d73938d3d273a75db671b0}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61aca2df47d5d42d73938d3d273a75db671b0}} 
ai\+Blend\+Mode\+\_\+\+Default&Formula\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{1}
\DoxyCodeLine{SourceColor*SourceAlpha + DestColor*(1-\/SourceAlpha)}

\end{DoxyCode}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiBlendMode\_Additive@{aiBlendMode\_Additive}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiBlendMode\_Additive@{aiBlendMode\_Additive}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61aca60eb5958c8fd4147bafd9098edf54e1e}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_ae1236da1ccfbf4f23bb490287a4d61aca60eb5958c8fd4147bafd9098edf54e1e}}

@code
SourceColor*1 + DestColor*1

\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cf}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cf}} 
\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiShadingMode@{aiShadingMode}}
\index{aiShadingMode@{aiShadingMode}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiShadingMode}{aiShadingMode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cf}{ai\+Shading\+Mode}}}



Defines all shading models supported by the library. 

Property\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a0f7ec9923cf262ba5b74d3c52bc588a1}{AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+SHADING\+\_\+\+MODEL}}

The list of shading modes has been taken from Blender. See Blender documentation for more information. The API does not distinguish between \char`\"{}specular\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}diffuse\char`\"{} shaders (thus the specular term for diffuse shading models like Oren-\/\+Nayar remains undefined). ~\newline
 Again, this value is just a hint. \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} tries to select the shader whose most common implementation matches the original rendering results of the 3D modeler which wrote a particular model as closely as possible. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiShadingMode\_Flat@{aiShadingMode\_Flat}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiShadingMode\_Flat@{aiShadingMode\_Flat}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cfa59fa2c27721e28dadd58cbd39cd46782}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cfa59fa2c27721e28dadd58cbd39cd46782}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiShadingMode\_PBR\_BRDF@{aiShadingMode\_PBR\_BRDF}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiShadingMode\_PBR\_BRDF@{aiShadingMode\_PBR\_BRDF}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cfa0b3fe30914cb8961c68b0faa888a8be1}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a93e23e0201d6ed86fb4287e15218e4cfa0b3fe30914cb8961c68b0faa888a8be1}} 
ai\+Shading\+Mode\+\_\+\+PBR\+\_\+\+BRDF&Physically-\/\+Based Rendering (PBR) shading using Bidirectional scattering/reflectance distribution function (BSDF/\+BRDF) There are multiple methods under this banner, and model files may provide data for more than one PBR-\/\+BRDF method. Applications should use the set of provided properties to determine which of their preferred PBR rendering methods are likely to be available eg\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+METALLIC\+\_\+\+FACTOR is set, then a Metallic/\+Roughness is available
\item If AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+GLOSSINESS\+\_\+\+FACTOR is set, then a Specular/\+Glossiness is available Note that some PBR methods allow layering of techniques 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

ai\+Shading\+Mode\+\_\+\+PBR\+\_\+\+BRDF&Physically-\/\+Based Rendering (PBR) shading using Bidirectional scattering/reflectance distribution function (BSDF/\+BRDF) There are multiple methods under this banner, and model files may provide data for more than one PBR-\/\+BRDF method. Applications should use the set of provided properties to determine which of their preferred PBR rendering methods are likely to be available eg\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+METALLIC\+\_\+\+FACTOR is set, then a Metallic/\+Roughness is available
\item If AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+GLOSSINESS\+\_\+\+FACTOR is set, then a Specular/\+Glossiness is available Note that some PBR methods allow layering of techniques 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureFlags@{aiTextureFlags}}
\index{aiTextureFlags@{aiTextureFlags}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiTextureFlags}{aiTextureFlags}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfd}{ai\+Texture\+Flags}}}



Defines some mixed flags for a particular texture. 

Usually you\textquotesingle{}ll instruct your cg artists how textures have to look like ... and how they will be processed in your application. However, if you use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} for completely generic loading purposes you might also need to process these flags in order to display as many \textquotesingle{}unknown\textquotesingle{} 3D models as possible correctly.

This corresponds to the \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a69577e4366cceb502288474cf8cf2dab}{AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+TEXFLAGS}} property. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureFlags\_Invert@{aiTextureFlags\_Invert}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureFlags\_Invert@{aiTextureFlags\_Invert}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda2d22809697f40ef1969a491a8d3278ff}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda2d22809697f40ef1969a491a8d3278ff}} 
ai\+Texture\+Flags\+\_\+\+Invert&The texture\textquotesingle{}s color values have to be inverted (component-\/wise 1-\/n) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureFlags\_UseAlpha@{aiTextureFlags\_UseAlpha}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureFlags\_UseAlpha@{aiTextureFlags\_UseAlpha}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda5712da7264ec0c6e90b45580e5badbe0}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda5712da7264ec0c6e90b45580e5badbe0}} 
ai\+Texture\+Flags\+\_\+\+Use\+Alpha&Explicit request to the application to process the alpha channel of the texture.

Mutually exclusive with \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda78f2667e8304213210c2508b7af47499}{ai\+Texture\+Flags\+\_\+\+Ignore\+Alpha}}. These flags are set if the library can say for sure that the alpha channel is used/is not used. If the model format does not define this, it is left to the application to decide whether the texture alpha channel -\/ if any -\/ is evaluated or not. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureFlags\_IgnoreAlpha@{aiTextureFlags\_IgnoreAlpha}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureFlags\_IgnoreAlpha@{aiTextureFlags\_IgnoreAlpha}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda78f2667e8304213210c2508b7af47499}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda78f2667e8304213210c2508b7af47499}} 
ai\+Texture\+Flags\+\_\+\+Ignore\+Alpha&Explicit request to the application to ignore the alpha channel of the texture.

Mutually exclusive with \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6d003e078617e4e80d1313a6250b2dfda5712da7264ec0c6e90b45580e5badbe0}{ai\+Texture\+Flags\+\_\+\+Use\+Alpha}}. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9}} 
\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureMapping@{aiTextureMapping}}
\index{aiTextureMapping@{aiTextureMapping}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiTextureMapping}{aiTextureMapping}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9}{ai\+Texture\+Mapping}}}



Defines how the mapping coords for a texture are generated. 

Real-\/time applications typically require full UV coordinates, so the use of the ai\+Process\+\_\+\+Gen\+UVCoords step is highly recommended. It generates proper UV channels for non-\/\+UV mapped objects, as long as an accurate description how the mapping should look like (e.\+g spherical) is given. See the \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_af72d0714d106aa52da2dbdf10d975c54}{AI\+\_\+\+MATKEY\+\_\+\+MAPPING}} property for more details. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureMapping\_UV@{aiTextureMapping\_UV}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureMapping\_UV@{aiTextureMapping\_UV}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9afe4af8e2f0303198ff2c51edf3039277}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9afe4af8e2f0303198ff2c51edf3039277}} 
ai\+Texture\+Mapping\+\_\+\+UV&The mapping coordinates are taken from an UV channel. \begin{DoxyVerb}#AI_MATKEY_UVWSRC property specifies from which UV channel
the texture coordinates are to be taken from (remember,
meshes can have more than one UV channel).
\end{DoxyVerb}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6b}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6b}} 
\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp@{aiTextureOp}}
\index{aiTextureOp@{aiTextureOp}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiTextureOp}{aiTextureOp}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6b}{ai\+Texture\+Op}}}



Defines how the Nth texture of a specific type is combined with the result of all previous layers. 

Example (left\+: key, right\+: value)\+: ~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{DiffColor0     -\/ gray}
\DoxyCodeLine{DiffTextureOp0 -\/ aiTextureOpMultiply}
\DoxyCodeLine{DiffTexture0   -\/ tex1.png}
\DoxyCodeLine{DiffTextureOp0 -\/ aiTextureOpAdd}
\DoxyCodeLine{DiffTexture1   -\/ tex2.png}

\end{DoxyCode}
 Written as equation, the final diffuse term for a specific pixel would be\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{diffFinal = DiffColor0 * sampleTex(DiffTexture0,UV0) +}
\DoxyCodeLine{   sampleTex(DiffTexture1,UV0) * diffContrib;}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where \textquotesingle{}diff\+Contrib\textquotesingle{} is the intensity of the incoming light for that pixel. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_Multiply@{aiTextureOp\_Multiply}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_Multiply@{aiTextureOp\_Multiply}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba4b4cf98920571bc5b5cdf333d1642759}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba4b4cf98920571bc5b5cdf333d1642759}} 
ai\+Texture\+Op\+\_\+\+Multiply&T = T1 $\ast$ T2 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_Add@{aiTextureOp\_Add}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_Add@{aiTextureOp\_Add}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba38c643dc19bdb5dad544c54829129d14}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba38c643dc19bdb5dad544c54829129d14}} 
ai\+Texture\+Op\+\_\+\+Add&T = T1 + T2 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_Subtract@{aiTextureOp\_Subtract}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_Subtract@{aiTextureOp\_Subtract}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6bac20a0da785e4670500e7338bc59a0793}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6bac20a0da785e4670500e7338bc59a0793}} 
ai\+Texture\+Op\+\_\+\+Subtract&T = T1 -\/ T2 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_Divide@{aiTextureOp\_Divide}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_Divide@{aiTextureOp\_Divide}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6bac15b6232b50780f509edf0a6b39af72c}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6bac15b6232b50780f509edf0a6b39af72c}} 
ai\+Texture\+Op\+\_\+\+Divide&T = T1 / T2 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_SmoothAdd@{aiTextureOp\_SmoothAdd}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_SmoothAdd@{aiTextureOp\_SmoothAdd}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba174eaa1b84bdcc131febea53da22aa4a}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6ba174eaa1b84bdcc131febea53da22aa4a}} 
ai\+Texture\+Op\+\_\+\+Smooth\+Add&T = (T1 + T2) -\/ (T1 $\ast$ T2) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureOp\_SignedAdd@{aiTextureOp\_SignedAdd}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureOp\_SignedAdd@{aiTextureOp\_SignedAdd}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6babe30ac3d3c7bff0fe1d69c70fbd646ff}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6babe30ac3d3c7bff0fe1d69c70fbd646ff}}

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_source_l00081}{81}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_source}{material.\+h}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0}} 
\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureType@{aiTextureType}}
\index{aiTextureType@{aiTextureType}!material.h@{material.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiTextureType}{aiTextureType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0}{ai\+Texture\+Type}}}



Defines the purpose of a texture. 

This is a very difficult topic. Different 3D packages support different kinds of textures. For very common texture types, such as bumpmaps, the rendering results depend on implementation details in the rendering pipelines of these applications. \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} loads all texture references from the model file and tries to determine which of the predefined texture types below is the best choice to match the original use of the texture as closely as possible.~\newline


In content pipelines you\textquotesingle{}ll usually define how textures have to be handled, and the artists working on models have to conform to this specification, regardless which 3D tool they\textquotesingle{}re using. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureType\_NONE@{aiTextureType\_NONE}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureType\_NONE@{aiTextureType\_NONE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a29933480f8f018b381ae8be57435a435}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a29933480f8f018b381ae8be57435a435}} 
ai\+Texture\+Type\+\_\+\+NONE&Dummy value. \begin{DoxyVerb}No texture, but the value to be used as 'texture semantic'
(#aiMaterialProperty::mSemantic) for all material properties
*not* related to textures.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureType\_DIFFUSE@{aiTextureType\_DIFFUSE}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureType\_DIFFUSE@{aiTextureType\_DIFFUSE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a3027af56603d5babd7e2efcf5ed1debd}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a3027af56603d5babd7e2efcf5ed1debd}} 
ai\+Texture\+Type\+\_\+\+DIFFUSE&LEGACY API MATERIALS Legacy refers to materials which Were originally implemented in the specifications around 2000. These must never be removed, as most engines support them. The texture is combined with the result of the diffuse lighting equation. OR PBR Specular/\+Glossiness \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureType\_SHEEN@{aiTextureType\_SHEEN}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureType\_SHEEN@{aiTextureType\_SHEEN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a2534326d369dc2b340ac0c23a9405c0a}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a2534326d369dc2b340ac0c23a9405c0a}} 
ai\+Texture\+Type\+\_\+\+SHEEN&PBR \mbox{\hyperlink{class_material}{Material}} Modifiers Some modern renderers have further PBR modifiers that may be overlaid on top of the \textquotesingle{}base\textquotesingle{} PBR materials for additional realism. These use multiple texture maps, so only the base type is directly defined Sheen Generally used to simulate textiles that are covered in a layer of microfibers eg velvet \href{https://github.com/KhronosGroup/glTF/tree/master/extensions/2.0/Khronos/KHR_materials_sheen}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Khronos\+Group/gl\+TF/tree/master/extensions/2.\+0/\+Khronos/\+KHR\+\_\+materials\+\_\+sheen}} \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{aiTextureType\_SHEEN@{aiTextureType\_SHEEN}!material.h@{material.h}}\index{material.h@{material.h}!aiTextureType\_SHEEN@{aiTextureType\_SHEEN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a2534326d369dc2b340ac0c23a9405c0a}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0a2534326d369dc2b340ac0c23a9405c0a}} 
ai\+Texture\+Type\+\_\+\+SHEEN&PBR \mbox{\hyperlink{class_material}{Material}} Modifiers Some modern renderers have further PBR modifiers that may be overlaid on top of the \textquotesingle{}base\textquotesingle{} PBR materials for additional realism. These use multiple texture maps, so only the base type is directly defined Sheen Generally used to simulate textiles that are covered in a layer of microfibers eg velvet \href{https://github.com/KhronosGroup/glTF/tree/master/extensions/2.0/Khronos/KHR_materials_sheen}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Khronos\+Group/gl\+TF/tree/master/extensions/2.\+0/\+Khronos/\+KHR\+\_\+materials\+\_\+sheen}} \\

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} specStrength = 1.f; \textcolor{comment}{// default value, remains unmodified if we fail.}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_aa8c1788fd9d096036c9e3b6cfe4b1301}{C\+\_\+\+ENUM}} \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2types_8h_a1f78dfb65090aa930cabb984c8abe711}{ai\+Return}} ai\+Get\+Material\+Texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_material}{ai\+Material}} $\ast$}]{mat,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_aa8c1788fd9d096036c9e3b6cfe4b1301}{C\+\_\+\+ENUM}} \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a7dd415ff703a2cc53d1c22ddbbd7dde0}{ai\+Texture\+Type}}}]{type,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{index,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_string}{ai\+String}} $\ast$}]{path,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_aa8c1788fd9d096036c9e3b6cfe4b1301}{C\+\_\+\+ENUM}} \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6186e909f1ae28133ab10f1b4635b0f9}{ai\+Texture\+Mapping}} $\ast$}]{mapping,  }\item[{unsigned int $\ast$}]{uvindex,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_af221f9bbc3e0dc43a46efaaac6dab067}{ai\+\_\+real}} $\ast$}]{blend,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_aa8c1788fd9d096036c9e3b6cfe4b1301}{C\+\_\+\+ENUM}} \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_afcd3096d69affba13114cedfc6f9ee6b}{ai\+Texture\+Op}} $\ast$}]{op,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2defs_8h_aa8c1788fd9d096036c9e3b6cfe4b1301}{C\+\_\+\+ENUM}} \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a6cbe56056751aa80e8dd714632a49de0}{ai\+Texture\+Map\+Mode}} $\ast$}]{mapmode,  }\item[{unsigned int $\ast$}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Helper function to get all values pertaining to a particular texture slot from a material structure. 

This function is provided just for convenience. You could also read the texture by parsing all of its properties manually. This function bundles all of them in a huge function monster.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em mat} & Pointer to the input material. May not be NULL \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type} & Specifies the texture stack to read from (e.\+g. diffuse, specular, height map ...). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em index} & Index of the texture. The function fails if the requested index is not available for this texture type. \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a8d331464c4f86b44cb6c6d64e39398ed}{ai\+Get\+Material\+Texture\+Count()}} can be used to determine the number of textures in a particular texture stack. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em path} & Receives the output path If the texture is embedded, receives a \textquotesingle{}$\ast$\textquotesingle{} followed by the id of the texture (for the textures stored in the corresponding scene) which can be converted to an int using a function like atoi. This parameter must be non-\/null. \\
\hline
 & {\em mapping} & The texture mapping mode to be used. Pass NULL if you\textquotesingle{}re not interested in this information. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em uvindex} & For UV-\/mapped textures\+: receives the index of the UV source channel. Unmodified otherwise. Pass NULL if you\textquotesingle{}re not interested in this information. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em blend} & Receives the blend factor for the texture Pass NULL if you\textquotesingle{}re not interested in this information. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em op} & Receives the texture blend operation to be perform between this texture and the previous texture. Pass NULL if you\textquotesingle{}re not interested in this information. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em mapmode} & Receives the mapping modes to be used for the texture. Pass NULL if you\textquotesingle{}re not interested in this information. Otherwise, pass a pointer to an array of two ai\+Texture\+Map\+Mode\textquotesingle{}s (one for each axis, UV order). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em flags} & Receives the the texture flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
AI\+\_\+\+SUCCESS on success, otherwise something else. Have fun. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a8d331464c4f86b44cb6c6d64e39398ed}\label{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_a8d331464c4f86b44cb6c6d64e39398ed}}

Get the number of textures for a particular texture type. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+Mat} & Pointer to the input material. May not be NULL \\
\hline
 & {\em type} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_texture}{Texture}} type to check for \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Number of textures for this type. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A texture can be easily queried using \mbox{\hyperlink{thirdparty_2assimp_2include_2assimp_2_material_8h_af3a53df46231d9f0aab39e972cd40ad3}{ai\+Get\+Material\+Texture()}} 
\end{DoxyNote}
